```python


# DO NOT RUN THIS CELL
# Customization

color = 'insert column name'    
point = 'True'                  
bin = 'True'
tooltip = 'insert column name'

#https://altair-viz.github.io/

# Charts

.mark_bar()              bar chart
.mark_rect()             heatmap
.mark_bar(), bin = True  histogram
.mark_line()             line chart
.mark_circle/point()     scatterplot
.mark_tick()             strip plot
.mark_area()             area chart
.mark_shape()            geolocation
.mark_rule()             boxplot


Bar Chart - Good for nominal and small ordinal categorical data.
Line Chart - Good for ordinal categorical and interval data.
Area Chart - Good for interval data.
Scatter Plot - Good for interval and some nominal categorical data.

```

        .mark_bar()              bar chart
        ^
    SyntaxError: invalid syntax




```python
# libraries

import pandas as pd
import altair as alt
```


```python
url = 'https://gist.githubusercontent.com/curran/a08a1080b88344b0c8a7/raw/d546eaee765268bf2f487608c537c05e22e4b221/iris.csv'
df = pd.read_csv(url)
# Dataset is now stored in a Pandas Dataframe
```

```python
# Bar Chat

alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_bar().encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length'),
    y='count()',
      tooltip = 'sepal_length'
  
)

chart
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
#by color

# Bar Chat - Good for nominal and small ordinal categorical data.

alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_bar().encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length'),
    y='count()',
    color='sepal_length',
    tooltip = 'sepal_length'
)

chart
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
#Scatterplot with Filter


input_dropdown = alt.binding_select(options=['setosa','versicolor','virginica'])
selection = alt.selection_single(fields=['species'], bind=input_dropdown, name='Filter')


alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_point().encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_width'),
    y=alt.Y('sepal_length'),
    color='species',
    tooltip = 'species',
    
).add_selection(
    selection
).transform_filter(
    selection
)
 
chart
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
# Hisotgram - With Scales

scales = alt.selection_interval(bind='scales')


alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_bar().encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length',bin =True),
    y='count()',
    color='sepal_length',
    tooltip = 'sepal_length'
).add_selection(
    scales
)

chart
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
#Heatmap


scales = alt.selection_interval(bind='scales')


alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_rect().encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length'),
    y=alt.Y('sepal_width'),
    color='sepal_length',
    tooltip = 'sepal_length',
    
).add_selection(
    scales
)
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
#Line Chart




alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_line(point=True).encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length'),
    y=alt.Y('sepal_width'),
    color='sepal_length',
    tooltip = 'sepal_length'
    

)
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'

      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
#Strip Plot




alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_tick(point=True).encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length'),
    y=alt.Y('sepal_width'),
    color='sepal_length',
    tooltip = 'sepal_length'
    

)
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'

```python
#Area chart

    x=alt.X('sepal_length'),
```

      function showError(el, error){

        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
#Heatmap binned


scales = alt.selection_interval(bind='scales')


alt.data_transformers.enable('default', max_rows=None)

# plot the dataset, referencing dataframe column names
import altair as alt
chart = alt.Chart(df).mark_rect().encode(
    x=alt.X('sepal_length', bin=alt.Bin(maxbins=60)),
    y=alt.Y('sepal_width', bin=alt.Bin(maxbins=60)),
    color='sepal_length',
    tooltip = 'sepal_length',
    
).add_selection(
    scales
)

chart
```

      var embedOpt = {"mode": "vega-lite"};

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
      }
      const el = document.getElementById('altair-viz');
      vegaEmbed("#altair-viz", spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(error => showError(el, error));

```python
# Line Chart with Date data - changed datasource
import altair as alt
from vega_datasets import data

source = data.stocks()

alt.Chart(source).mark_line().encode(
    x='date',
    y='price',
    color='symbol'
)
```

      function showError(el, error){
          el.innerHTML = ('<div class="error" style="color:red;">'
                          + '<p>JavaScript Error: ' + error.message + '</p>'
                          + "<p>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. "
                          + "See the javascript console for the full traceback.</p>"
                          + '</div>');
          throw error;
